							OR = {
								is_rival = ROOT
								is_enemy = ROOT
							}
							
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					event_target:wants_unite_EU = {
						NOT = {	capital_scope = { same_continent = ROOT } }
						is_neighbor_of = ROOT
						NOT = { alliance_with = ROOT }
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.25
					event_target:wants_unite_EU = {
						war_with = ROOT
						is_hiring_condottiere_from = event_target:wants_unite_EU
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.05
					OR = {
						ruler_has_personality = babbling_buffoon_personality
						ruler_has_personality = embezzler_personality
						ruler_has_personality = infertile_personality
						ruler_has_personality = drunkard_personality
						ruler_has_personality = sinner_personality
						ruler_has_personality = greedy_personality
						ruler_has_personality = cruel_personality
						ruler_has_personality = naive_personality
						ruler_has_personality = craven_personality
						ruler_has_personality = loose_lips_personality
						ruler_has_personality = obsessive_perfectionist_personality
						ruler_has_personality = malevolent_personality
					}
					
					
				}
			}
    		add_adm_power = -100
			add_dip_power = -100
			add_mil_power = -100
    		reverse_add_opinion = {
    		    who = event_target:wants_unite_EU
    		    modifier = mini_bad_relation
    		}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					has_country_flag = show_EU_vote
				}
				country_event = {
					id = european_union_vote_unite.15 days = 1
				}
			}
    		hidden_effect = {
    		    event_target:wants_unite_EU = {
					country_event = {
						id = set_variable.38 days = 2
					}
				}
    		    event_target:wants_unite_EU = { 
    		        change_variable = {
    		            which = VETO_on_EU_Metting
    		            value = 1
    		        }
    		    }
    		    if = {
    		        limit = {
    		            ai = yes
    		        }
    		        add_country_modifier = {
    		            name = cool_down_veto
    		            duration = 3650
    		        }
    		    }
    		    if = {
    		        limit = {
    		            ai = no
    		        }
    		        add_country_modifier = {
    		            name = cool_down_veto
    		            duration = 730
    		        }
    		    }
    		}
			
		}
	}
